[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m187[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m190[0m[39m:#  define [0m[1;35mmsan_unpoison[0m[1;39m([0m[39mr, s[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35m__msan_unpoison[0m[1;39m([0m[39mr, s[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m192[0m[39m:#  define [0m[1;35mmsan_unpoison[0m[1;39m([0m[39mr, s[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m193[0m[39m:#endif[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m194[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m195[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m* Dummy allocator to tell the compiler that the new size of p is newsize. The [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation returns the[0m                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m197[0m[39m: * be inlined [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhence a non-static function with _noinline_ because LTO [0m         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m198[0m[39m: * gcc then loses the attributes on the function.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m199[0m[39m: * See: [0m[4;94mhttps://gcc.gnu.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?[0m[4;94mid[0m[4;94m=[0m[4;94m96503[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m200[0m[39m:void *[0m[1;35mexpand_to_usable[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid *p, size_t newsize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35m_alloc_[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m _returns_nonnull_ [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m_noinline_;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:        q = [0m[1;35mrealloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*p, newalloc[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m160[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35massert[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpayload[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m161[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35massert[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpayload_size > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m162[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpayload[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY%[0m[1;36m10[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m[32m'0'[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m163[0m[39m:                payload[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY*[0m[1;36m100[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m164[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The out-of-bounds write originates in `finish_item` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcatalog.[0m[1;92mc:162[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m164[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, where[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma testing macro [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m causes an unconditional write to [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`payload[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY*[0m[1;36m100[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` without any bounds check. Since `payload` is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtypically only allocated in [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m-byte increments [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia `GREEDY_REALLOC`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and may be [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfar smaller than `ILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY*[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m`, this triggers a one-byte [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap-buffer-overflow.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The write is purely a debug/fuzzing helper [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtriggering corruption when [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`payload[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` matches a test digit[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and is not part of production catalog logic. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRemoving or guarding it does not affect the catalog parsing or storage semantics.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All legitimate catalog-building logic in `finish_item` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcreation of [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CatalogItem`, combining entries, insertion into `OrderedHashmap`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntouched.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The payload accumulation and null-termination at its natural end [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`payload[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpayload_size[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is preserved.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness, fuzzing entry point, or tests are modified; this patch only alters[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproduction code.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Steps[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `src/libsystemd/sd-journal/catalog.c`, locate the start of `finish_item`:[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        static int [0m[1;35mfinish_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mOrderedHashmap *h, sd_id128_t id, const char [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*language, char *payload, size_t payload_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Remove lines [0m[1;36m161[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m164[0m[39m, i.e. the entire conditional block:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpayload[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY%[0m[1;36m10[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m[32m'0'[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                payload[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY*[0m[1;36m100[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Keep the assertions and all subsequent logic unchanged:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35massert[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpayload[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35massert[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpayload_size > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[33m...[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrest of finish_item[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Re-compile and re-run `fuzz-catalog` to verify that the heap-buffer-overflow [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis eliminated and no regressions in functionality occur.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Rationale and Side-Effect Mitigation[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By removing this debug write, we eliminate the unchecked OOB write that was [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggering ASan failures.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - There is no loss of user-visible functionality, since `ILLEGAL_CAT_ENTRY` was [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monly intended for fuzz-based error injection.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other code paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., normal null-termination, merging of payloads, language[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are unaffected.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If in the future a safe test-injection mechanism is desired, it should [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexplicitly check `idx < payload_size` before writing.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. References[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar test-only code patterns are excluded from production in other [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubsystems of systemd to avoid unchecked memory writes [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., debug assertion [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhelpers guarded by `#if DEBUG`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `GREEDY_REALLOC` logic already ensures payload buffers are grown safely; [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno changes to memory-allocation utilities are needed.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>src/libsystemd/sd-journal/catalog.[0m[1;92mc:160[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m164[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
